    <script>
     /*variable*/
      let focusinit = document.querySelectorAll('.site-header__logo-wrapper')[0];
      focusinit.setAttribute('tabindex','-1');
     
      /*focus in element logo */

     function timefocus_init(){

       let focus_interval = setTimeout(focustime,3000);

     };
    
      function focustime() {
         focusinit.focus();
       };
      
       timefocus_init();
    </script>

   <!-- insert auto focus with modal -->
   <script>
    let focusedElementBeforeModal;
  const modal = document.querySelector('.modal');
  let btn_close = document.querySelector('.modal__close');

  let modalToggle = document.querySelector('#menu-item-77');

  modalToggle.addEventListener('click', openModalGetStarted);
  
  function openModalGetStarted() {
    focusedElementBeforeModal = document.activeElement;

    modal.addEventListener('keydown', trapTabKey);

    // Listen Close button

    btn_close.addEventListener('keydown',(e)=>{ 

      if (e.keyCode === 13 ) {
        e.preventDefault();
      modal.classList.remove('modal--is-open');
      focusedElementBeforeModal.focus();
    }
    });

    let focusableElementsString = 'a[href], area[href], input:not([disabled]), select:not([disabled]), textarea:not([disabled]), button:not([disabled]), iframe, object, embed, [tabindex="0"], [contenteditable]';
    let focusableElements = modal.querySelectorAll(focusableElementsString);
    focusableElements = Array.prototype.slice.call(focusableElements);
    let familiesTab = focusableElements[1];
    familiesTab.setAttribute('tabindex','0');
    let firstTabStop = focusableElements[0];
    let lastTabStop = focusableElements[focusableElements.length - 1];
    
    setTimeout(()=>{ 
        firstTabStop.focus();
    }, 1000);

    function trapTabKey(e) {
      if (e.keyCode === 9) {
        if (e.shiftKey) {
          if (document.activeElement === firstTabStop) {
            e.preventDefault();
            lastTabStop.focus();
          }
        } else {
          if (document.activeElement === lastTabStop) {
            e.preventDefault();
            firstTabStop.focus();
          }
        }
      }
    }
      
  }
   </script>

   <script>
    (function($) {
    // scrolling on load
    $(window).bind("load", function() {
        var win = $(window),
            scrollContainer = $('.scroller'),
            scrollImages = $('.scroller__col--images'),
            headerHeight = $('.header').outerHeight(),
            unFixContainerOffset = (scrollContainer.offset().top + scrollContainer.height()) - win.height(),
            scrollCopyBlocks = $('.scroller__copy');

        for(var i = 0; i < scrollCopyBlocks.length; i++) {
            var j = i + 1,
                scrollBlock = $(scrollCopyBlocks[i]);
                scrollBlock.attr('data-info', '#scroller__image--'+j);
        }

        $(window).scroll(function () {
            for(var i = 0; i < scrollCopyBlocks.length; i++) {
                var scrollBlock = $(scrollCopyBlocks[i]);

                var sectionTop = scrollBlock.offset().top,
                    scrollImageItem = scrollBlock.attr('data-info');
                //if we're visible
                if ( (win.scrollTop() + (win.height() /2 )) > sectionTop ) {
                    $(scrollImageItem).addClass('current');
                }
                else {
                    $(scrollImageItem).removeClass('current');
                }
            }
        });

        $(window).scroll(function() {
            if(win.scrollTop() > scrollContainer.offset().top && win.scrollTop() < unFixContainerOffset ) {
                scrollImages.addClass('fixed');
            }
            else {
                scrollImages.removeClass('fixed');
            }

            if(win.scrollTop() > unFixContainerOffset ) {
                scrollImages.addClass('fix-absolute-left');
            }
            else {
                scrollImages.removeClass('fix-absolute-left');
            }

        });
    });

    // scrolling on resize
    $(window).bind("resize", function() {
        var win = $(window),
            scrollContainer = $('.scroller'),
            scrollImages = $('.scroller__col--images'),
            headerHeight = $('.header').outerHeight(),
            unFixContainerOffset = (scrollContainer.offset().top + scrollContainer.height()) - win.height(),
            scrollCopyBlocks = $('.scroller__copy');

        for(var i = 0; i < scrollCopyBlocks.length; i++) {
            var j = i + 1,
                scrollBlock = $(scrollCopyBlocks[i]);
                scrollBlock.attr('data-info', '#scroller__image--'+j);
        }

        $(window).scroll(function () {
            for(var i = 0; i < scrollCopyBlocks.length; i++) {
                var scrollBlock = $(scrollCopyBlocks[i]);

                var sectionTop = scrollBlock.offset().top,
                    scrollImageItem = scrollBlock.attr('data-info');
                //if we're visible
                if ( (win.scrollTop() + (win.height() /2 )) > sectionTop ) {
                    $(scrollImageItem).addClass('current');
                }
                else {
                    $(scrollImageItem).removeClass('current');
                }
            }
        });

        $(window).scroll(function() {
            if(win.scrollTop() > scrollContainer.offset().top && win.scrollTop() < unFixContainerOffset ) {
                scrollImages.addClass('fixed');
            }
            else {
                scrollImages.removeClass('fixed');
            }

            if(win.scrollTop() > unFixContainerOffset ) {
                scrollImages.addClass('fix-absolute-left');
            }
            else {
                scrollImages.removeClass('fix-absolute-left');
            }

        });
    });
    var isDesktop = $(window).width() > 767;

    $(window).on('resize', function() {

        if (isDesktop && $(window).width() < 768) {
            isDesktop = false;
            window.location.reload();
        } else if (!isDesktop && $(window).width() > 767) {
            isDesktop = true;
            window.location.reload();
        }
    });
}(jQuery));
   </script>
